			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

			</div> -->

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

			</div> -->

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

			</div> -->

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

			</div> -->

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

			</div> -->

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">
				<p class="meta">
				Posted: <br />
				Tags: <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/tag/unix/" rel="tag">UNIX</a> 								</p>
			</div> -->

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

			</div> -->

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

			</div> -->

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">
				<p class="meta">
				Posted: <br />
				Tags: <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/tag/unix/" rel="tag">UNIX</a> 								</p>
			</div> -->

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			</div> -->

			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />

				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

			</div> -->

			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />

                <div id="first-300-ad">

<script type="text/javascript">

<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			</div> -->

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

			</div> -->

<ul id="navigation-left">
 <li><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com" title="" class="win"><h3>CATEGORIES</h3></a></li>
 
 
             
  
  
    
  
                  <li class="current"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/">UNIX</a></li>

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

	<div id="content_internal">

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

			</div> -->

			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

		<div class="post" id="post-220">
		
		  
			<div class="post-content-internal">
			<!-- google_ad_section_start --> 
				<h2 class="storytitle"><a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" rel="bookmark">Search for text in vi or vim</a></h2>
				<img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/user-icon.jpg" alt="Contributor Icon" class="icon" />
                <em class="contributor">Contributed by <a href="/author/Rex/">Rex</a></em> <img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/date-icon.jpg" alt="Date Icon" class="icon date" />
				November 10, 2003 &nbsp;<BR> <script type="text/javascript">SHARETHIS.addEntry({ title: "Search for text in vi or vim", url: "http://www.tech-recipes.com/rx/220/search-for-text-in-vi-or-vim/" });</script>                <span class="tags"><img src="http://m.tech-recipes.com/t/tag-icon.jpg" alt="Tag Icon" class="icon" /> <strong>Tagged:</strong>  <a href="http://www.tech-recipes.com/category/unix/" title="View all posts in UNIX" rel="category tag">UNIX</a> </span>

                <div id="first-300-ad">
                	  <!-- begin ad tag (techrecipes/unix;300x250,336x280) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

ord = window.ord || Math.floor(Math.random()*1E16);

document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/adj/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=' + ord + '?"><\/script>');

//]]>

</script>
<noscript><a href="http://ad2.netshelter.net/jump/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=300x250,336x280;ord=123456789?" target="_blank" ><img src="http://ad2.netshelter.net/ad/ns.techrecipes/unix;kw=;tile=2;sz=728x90;ord=123456789?" border="0" alt="" /></a></noscript>
<!-- end ad tag -->                </div>
               
				<h4>vi and vim have powerful searching capabilities because they bring to bear the richness of regular expressions.  </h4>
<p><span id="more-220"></span><br />
To search for the next occurence of the text &#8216;maybe&#8217; from the current cursor position, type:</p>

<p><code>/maybe<ENTER><br />
</code></p>
<p>Search backward from the current position by using <strong>?</strong> instead of <strong>/</strong> in the command.  </p>
<p>Once you have searched for something, you can find the next occurrence by pressing <strong>n</strong> or the previous occurrence with <strong>N</strong>.  </p>

<p>Searching in vi/vim is enhanced with regular expressions.  For example, to find the next occurence of the text &#8216;Total&#8217; that occurs at the beginning of a line, use:</p>
<p><code>/^Total</code></p>
				<!-- google_ad_section_end -->
			</div>

			<!-- <div class="post-details">

			</div> -->
